I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
`<select>` doesn't respect `selected` attribute when spreading props
### Describe the bug

When you have a basic select tag, and give it an {...others} spread (like it's in a component and receives some properties), it will no longer show any option, regardless of it having the 'selected' property or not.

I linked the playground repro, but just to have it here as well, because it's so simple to visualize:

```svelte
<script>
	let others = {onclick: ()=> console.log('aaa')}
</script>

<select>
	<option>o1</option>
	<option selected>o2</option>
</select>

<select {...others}>
	<option>o1</option>
	<option selected>o2</option>
</select>
```

First select will have 'o2' selected, which is correct, the second select will have nothing selected. Only by removing the spread 'others' will it work again. Clicking on it will print the console, so the spread itself is working.

I'm not exactly sure when this started happening. I keep rolling back versions of svelte to no avail, but I know it definitely worked a few weeks ago when my full pipeline ran. I put "blocking an upgrade" because I will definitely revert to a working version once I... you know... actually find it.

### Reproduction

https://svelte.dev/playground/187497f0959046c19ab25f2129e9a3ae?version=latest


    28	/**
    29	 * @param {AST.RegularElement} node
    30	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    31	 */
    32	export function RegularElement(node, context) {
    33	        context.state.template.push_element(node.name, node.start);
    34	
    35	        if (node.name === 'noscript') {
    36	                context.state.template.pop_element();
    37	                return;
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        const is_custom_element = is_custom_element_node(node);
    41	
    42	        // cloneNode is faster, but it does not instantiate the underlying class of the
    43	        // custom element until the template is connected to the dom, which would
    44	        // cause problems when setting properties on the custom element.
    45	        // Therefore we need to use importNode instead, which doesn't have this caveat.
    46	        // Additionally, Webkit browsers need importNode for video elements for autoplay
    47	        // to work correctly.
    48	        context.state.template.needs_import_node ||= node.name === 'video' || is_custom_element;
    49	
    50	        context.state.template.contains_script_tag ||= node.name === 'script';
    51	
    52	        /** @type {Array<AST.Attribute | AST.SpreadAttribute>} */
    53	        const attributes = [];
    54	
    55	        /** @type {AST.ClassDirective[]} */
    56	        const class_directives = [];
    57	
    58	        /** @type {AST.StyleDirective[]} */
    59	        const style_directives = [];
    60	
    61	        /** @type {Array<AST.AnimateDirective | AST.BindDirective | AST.OnDirective | AST.TransitionDirective | AST.UseDirective | AST.AttachTag>} */
    62	        const other_directives = [];
    63	
    64	        /** @type {ExpressionStatement[]} */
    65	        const lets = [];
    66	
    67	        /** @type {Map<string, AST.Attribute>} */
    68	        const lookup = new Map();
    69	
    70	        /** @type {Map<string, AST.BindDirective>} */
    71	        const bindings = new Map();
    72	
    73	        let has_spread = node.metadata.has_spread;
    74	        let has_use = false;
    75	
    76	        for (const attribute of node.attributes) {
    77	                switch (attribute.type) {
    78	                        case 'AnimateDirective':
    79	                                other_directives.push(attribute);
    80	                                break;
    81	
    82	                        case 'Attribute':
    83	                                // `is` attributes need to be part of the template, otherwise they break
    84	                                if (attribute.name === 'is' && context.state.metadata.namespace === 'html') {
    85	                                        const { value } = build_attribute_value(attribute.value, context);
    86	
    87	                                        if (value.type === 'Literal' && typeof value.value === 'string') {
    88	                                                context.state.template.set_prop('is', value.value);
    89	                                                continue;
    90	                                        }
    91	                                }
    92	
    93	                                attributes.push(attribute);
    94	                                lookup.set(attribute.name, attribute);
    95	                                break;
    96	
    97	                        case 'BindDirective':
    98	                                bindings.set(attribute.name, attribute);
    99	                                other_directives.push(attribute);
   100	                                break;
   101	
   102	                        case 'ClassDirective':
   103	                                class_directives.push(attribute);
   104	                                break;
   105	
   106	                        case 'LetDirective':
   107	                                // visit let directives before everything else, to set state
   108	                                lets.push(/** @type {ExpressionStatement} */ (context.visit(attribute)));
   109	                                break;
   110	
   111	                        case 'OnDirective':
   112	                                other_directives.push(attribute);
   113	                                break;
   114	
   115	                        case 'SpreadAttribute':
   116	                                attributes.push(attribute);
   117	                                break;
   118	
   119	                        case 'StyleDirective':
   120	                                style_directives.push(attribute);
   121	                                break;
   122	
   123	                        case 'TransitionDirective':
   124	                                other_directives.push(attribute);
   125	                                break;
   126	
   127	                        case 'UseDirective':
   128	                                has_use = true;
   129	                                other_directives.push(attribute);
   130	                                break;
   131	
   132	                        case 'AttachTag':
   133	                                other_directives.push(attribute);
   134	                                break;
   135	                }
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        /** @type {typeof state} */
   139	        const element_state = { ...context.state, init: [], after_update: [] };
   140	
   141	        for (const attribute of other_directives) {
   142	                if (attribute.type === 'OnDirective') {
   143	                        const handler = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(attribute));
   144	
   145	                        if (has_use) {
   146	                                element_state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.effect', b.thunk(handler))));
   147	                        } else {
   148	                                element_state.after_update.push(b.stmt(handler));
   149	                        }
   150	                } else {
   151	                        context.visit(attribute, element_state);
   152	                }
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        if (node.name === 'input') {
   156	                const has_value_attribute = attributes.some(
   157	                        (attribute) =>
   158	                                attribute.type === 'Attribute' &&
   159	                                (attribute.name === 'value' || attribute.name === 'checked') &&
   160	                                !is_text_attribute(attribute)
   161	                );
   162	                const has_default_value_attribute = attributes.some(
   163	                        (attribute) =>
   164	                                attribute.type === 'Attribute' &&
   165	                                (attribute.name === 'defaultValue' || attribute.name === 'defaultChecked')
   166	                );
   167	                if (
   168	                        !has_default_value_attribute &&
   169	                        (has_spread ||
   170	                                bindings.has('value') ||
   171	                                bindings.has('checked') ||
   172	                                bindings.has('group') ||
   173	                                (!bindings.has('group') && has_value_attribute))
   174	                ) {
   175	                        context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.remove_input_defaults', context.state.node)));
   176	                }
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        if (node.name === 'textarea') {
   180	                const attribute = lookup.get('value') ?? lookup.get('checked');
   181	                const needs_content_reset = attribute && !is_text_attribute(attribute);
   182	
   183	                if (has_spread || bindings.has('value') || needs_content_reset) {
   184	                        context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.remove_textarea_child', context.state.node)));
   185	                }
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        if (node.name === 'select' && bindings.has('value')) {
   189	                setup_select_synchronization(/** @type {AST.BindDirective} */ (bindings.get('value')), context);
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        // Let bindings first, they can be used on attributes
   193	        context.state.init.push(...lets);
   194	
   195	        const node_id = context.state.node;
   196	
   197	        /** If true, needs `__value` for inputs */
   198	        const needs_special_value_handling =
   199	                node.name === 'option' ||
   200	                node.name === 'select' ||
   201	                bindings.has('group') ||
   202	                bindings.has('checked');
   203	
   204	        if (has_spread) {
   205	                build_attribute_effect(attributes, class_directives, style_directives, context, node, node_id);
   206	        } else {
   207	                for (const attribute of /** @type {AST.Attribute[]} */ (attributes)) {
   208	                        if (is_event_attribute(attribute)) {
   209	                                visit_event_attribute(attribute, context);
   210	                                continue;
   211	                        }
   212	
   213	                        if (needs_special_value_handling && attribute.name === 'value') {
   214	                                continue;
   215	                        }
   216	
   217	                        const name = get_attribute_name(node, attribute);
   218	
   219	                        if (
   220	                                !is_custom_element &&
   221	                                !cannot_be_set_statically(attribute.name) &&
   222	                                (attribute.value === true || is_text_attribute(attribute)) &&
   223	                                (name !== 'class' || class_directives.length === 0) &&
   224	                                (name !== 'style' || style_directives.length === 0)
   225	                        ) {
   226	                                let value = is_text_attribute(attribute) ? attribute.value[0].data : true;
   227	
   228	                                if (name === 'class' && node.metadata.scoped && context.state.analysis.css.hash) {
   229	                                        if (value === true || value === '') {
   230	                                                value = context.state.analysis.css.hash;
   231	                                        } else {
   232	                                                value += ' ' + context.state.analysis.css.hash;
   233	                                        }
   234	                                }
   235	
   236	                                if (name !== 'class' || value) {
   237	                                        context.state.template.set_prop(
   238	                                                attribute.name,
   239	                                                is_boolean_attribute(name) && value === true ? undefined : value === true ? '' : value
   240	                                        );
   241	                                }
   242	                        } else if (name === 'autofocus') {
   243	                                let { value } = build_attribute_value(attribute.value, context);
   244	                                context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.autofocus', node_id, value)));
   245	                        } else if (name === 'class') {
   246	                                const is_html = context.state.metadata.namespace === 'html' && node.name !== 'svg';
   247	                                build_set_class(node, node_id, attribute, class_directives, context, is_html);
   248	                        } else if (name === 'style') {
   249	                                build_set_style(node_id, attribute, style_directives, context);
   250	                        } else if (is_custom_element) {
   251	                                build_custom_element_attribute_update_assignment(node_id, attribute, context);
   252	                        } else {
   253	                                const { value, has_state } = build_attribute_value(
   254	                                        attribute.value,
   255	                                        context,
   256	                                        (value, metadata) => (metadata.has_call ? context.state.memoizer.add(value) : value)
   257	                                );
   258	
   259	                                const update = build_element_attribute_update(node, node_id, name, value, attributes);
   260	
   261	                                (has_state ? context.state.update : context.state.init).push(b.stmt(update));
   262	                        }
   263	                }
   264	        }
   265	
   266	        if (
   267	                is_load_error_element(node.name) &&
   268	                (has_spread || has_use || lookup.has('onload') || lookup.has('onerror'))
   269	        ) {
   270	                context.state.after_update.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.replay_events', node_id)));
   271	        }
   272	
   273	        const metadata = {
   274	                ...context.state.metadata,
   275	                namespace: determine_namespace_for_children(node, context.state.metadata.namespace)
   276	        };
   277	
   278	        if (bindings.has('innerHTML') || bindings.has('innerText') || bindings.has('textContent')) {
   279	                const contenteditable = lookup.get('contenteditable');
   280	
   281	                if (
   282	                        contenteditable &&
   283	                        (contenteditable.value === true ||
   284	                                (is_text_attribute(contenteditable) && contenteditable.value[0].data === 'true'))
   285	                ) {
   286	                        metadata.bound_contenteditable = true;
   287	                }
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        /** @type {ComponentClientTransformState} */
   291	        const state = {
   292	                ...context.state,
   293	                metadata,
   294	                scope: /** @type {Scope} */ (context.state.scopes.get(node.fragment)),
   295	                preserve_whitespace:
   296	                        context.state.preserve_whitespace || node.name === 'pre' || node.name === 'textarea'
   297	        };
   298	
   299	        const { hoisted, trimmed } = clean_nodes(
   300	                node,
   301	                node.fragment.nodes,
   302	                context.path,
   303	                state.metadata.namespace,
   304	                state,
   305	                node.name === 'script' || state.preserve_whitespace,
   306	                state.options.preserveComments
   307	        );
   308	
   309	        /** @type {typeof state} */
   310	        const child_state = { ...state, init: [], update: [], after_update: [] };
   311	
   312	        for (const node of hoisted) {
   313	                context.visit(node, child_state);
   314	        }
   315	
   316	        // special case — if an element that only contains text, we don't need
   317	        // to descend into it if the text is non-reactive
   318	        // in the rare case that we have static text that can't be inlined
   319	        // (e.g. `<span>{location}</span>`), set `textContent` programmatically
   320	        const use_text_content =
   321	                trimmed.every((node) => node.type === 'Text' || node.type === 'ExpressionTag') &&
   322	                trimmed.every((node) => node.type === 'Text' || !node.metadata.expression.has_state) &&
   323	                trimmed.some((node) => node.type === 'ExpressionTag');
   324	
   325	        if (use_text_content) {
   326	                const { value } = build_template_chunk(trimmed, context, child_state);
   327	                const empty_string = value.type === 'Literal' && value.value === '';
   328	
   329	                if (!empty_string) {
   330	                        child_state.init.push(
   331	                                b.stmt(b.assignment('=', b.member(context.state.node, 'textContent'), value))
   332	                        );
   333	                }
   334	        } else {
   335	                /** @type {Expression} */
   336	                let arg = context.state.node;
   337	
   338	                // If `hydrate_node` is set inside the element, we need to reset it
   339	                // after the element has been hydrated
   340	                let needs_reset = trimmed.some((node) => node.type !== 'Text');
   341	
   342	                // The same applies if it's a `<template>` element, since we need to
   343	                // set the value of `hydrate_node` to `node.content`
   344	                if (node.name === 'template') {
   345	                        needs_reset = true;
   346	                        child_state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.hydrate_template', arg)));
   347	                        arg = b.member(arg, 'content');
   348	                }
   349	
   350	                process_children(trimmed, (is_text) => b.call('$.child', arg, is_text && b.true), true, {
   351	                        ...context,
   352	                        state: child_state
   353	                });
   354	
   355	                if (needs_reset) {
   356	                        child_state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.reset', context.state.node)));
   357	                }
   358	        }
   359	
   360	        if (node.fragment.nodes.some((node) => node.type === 'SnippetBlock')) {
   361	                // Wrap children in `{...}` to avoid declaration conflicts
   362	                context.state.init.push(
   363	                        b.block([
   364	                                ...child_state.init,
   365	                                ...element_state.init,
   366	                                child_state.update.length > 0 ? build_render_statement(child_state) : b.empty,
   367	                                ...child_state.after_update,
   368	                                ...element_state.after_update
   369	                        ])
   370	                );
   371	        } else if (node.fragment.metadata.dynamic) {
   372	                context.state.init.push(...child_state.init, ...element_state.init);
   373	                context.state.update.push(...child_state.update);
   374	                context.state.after_update.push(...child_state.after_update, ...element_state.after_update);
   375	        } else {
   376	                context.state.init.push(...element_state.init);
   377	                context.state.after_update.push(...element_state.after_update);
   378	        }
   379	
   380	        if (lookup.has('dir')) {
   381	                // This fixes an issue with Chromium where updates to text content within an element
   382	                // does not update the direction when set to auto. If we just re-assign the dir, this fixes it.
   383	                const dir = b.member(node_id, 'dir');
   384	                context.state.update.push(b.stmt(b.assignment('=', dir, dir)));
   385	        }
   386	
   387	        if (!has_spread && needs_special_value_handling) {
   388	                for (const attribute of /** @type {AST.Attribute[]} */ (attributes)) {
   389	                        if (attribute.name === 'value') {
   390	                                build_element_special_value_attribute(node.name, node_id, attribute, context);
   391	                                break;
   392	                        }
   393	                }
   394	        }
   395	
   396	        context.state.template.pop_element();
   397	}
   398	
   399	/**
   400	 * Special case: if we have a value binding on a select element, we need to set up synchronization
   401	 * between the value binding and inner signals, for indirect updates
   402	 * @param {AST.BindDirective} value_binding
   403	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   404	 */
   405	function setup_select_synchronization(value_binding, context) {
   406	        if (context.state.analysis.runes) return;
   407	
   408	        let bound = value_binding.expression;
   409	
   410	        if (bound.type === 'SequenceExpression') {
   411	                return;
   412	        }
   413	
   414	        while (bound.type === 'MemberExpression') {
   415	                bound = /** @type {Identifier | MemberExpression} */ (bound.object);
   416	        }
   417	
   418	        /** @type {string[]} */
   419	        const names = [];
   420	
   421	        for (const [name, refs] of context.state.scope.references) {
   422	                if (
   423	                        refs.length > 0 &&
   424	                        // prevent infinite loop
   425	                        name !== bound.name
   426	                ) {
   427	                        names.push(name);
   428	                }
   429	        }
   430	
   431	        const invalidator = b.call(
   432	                '$.invalidate_inner_signals',
   433	                b.thunk(
   434	                        b.block(
   435	                                names.map((name) => {
   436	                                        const serialized = build_getter(b.id(name), context.state);
   437	                                        return b.stmt(serialized);
   438	                                })
   439	                        )
   440	                )
   441	        );
   442	
   443	        context.state.init.push(
   444	                b.stmt(
   445	                        b.call(
   446	                                '$.template_effect',
   447	                                b.thunk(
   448	                                        b.block([b.stmt(/** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(bound))), b.stmt(invalidator)])
   449	                                )
   450	                        )
   451	                )
   452	        );
   453	}
   454	
   455	/**
   456	 * @param {AST.ClassDirective[]} class_directives
   457	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   458	 * @param {Memoizer} memoizer
   459	 * @return {ObjectExpression | Identifier}
   460	 */
   461	export function build_class_directives_object(
   462	        class_directives,
   463	        context,
   464	        memoizer = context.state.memoizer
   465	) {
   466	        let properties = [];
   467	        let has_call_or_state = false;
   468	
   469	        for (const d of class_directives) {
   470	                const expression = /** @type Expression */ (context.visit(d.expression));
   471	                properties.push(b.init(d.name, expression));
   472	                has_call_or_state ||= d.metadata.expression.has_call || d.metadata.expression.has_state;
   473	        }
   474	
   475	        const directives = b.object(properties);
   476	
   477	        return has_call_or_state ? memoizer.add(directives) : directives;
   478	}
   479	
   480	/**
   481	 * @param {AST.StyleDirective[]} style_directives
   482	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   483	 * @param {Memoizer} memoizer
   484	 * @return {ObjectExpression | ArrayExpression | Identifier}}
   485	 */
   486	export function build_style_directives_object(
   487	        style_directives,
   488	        context,
   489	        memoizer = context.state.memoizer
   490	) {
   491	        const normal = b.object([]);
   492	        const important = b.object([]);
   493	
   494	        let has_call_or_state = false;
   495	
   496	        for (const d of style_directives) {
   497	                const expression =
   498	                        d.value === true
   499	                                ? build_getter(b.id(d.name), context.state)
   500	                                : build_attribute_value(d.value, context).value;
   501	
   502	                const object = d.modifiers.includes('important') ? important : normal;
   503	                object.properties.push(b.init(d.name, expression));
   504	
   505	                has_call_or_state ||= d.metadata.expression.has_call || d.metadata.expression.has_state;
   506	        }
   507	
   508	        const directives = important.properties.length ? b.array([normal, important]) : normal;
   509	
   510	        return has_call_or_state ? memoizer.add(directives) : directives;
   511	}

   515	 * the init or the init and update arrays, dependin<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.    541	function build_element_attribute_update(element, node_id, name, value, attributes) {
   542	        if (name === 'muted') {
   543	                // Special case for Firefox who needs it set as a property in order to work
   544	                return b.assignment('=', b.member(node_id, b.id('muted')), value);
   545	        }
   546	
   547	        if (name === 'value') {
   548	                return b.call('$.set_value', node_id, value);
   549	        }
   550	
   551	        if (name === 'checked') {
   552	                return b.call('$.set_checked', node_id, value);
   553	        }
   554	
   555	        if (name === 'selected') {
   556	                return b.call('$.set_selected', node_id, value);
   557	        }
   558	
   559	        if (
   560	                // If we would just set the defaultValue property, it would override the value property,
   561	                // because it is set in the template which implicitly means it's also setting the default value,
   562	                // and if one updates the default value while the input is pristine it will also update the
   563	                // current value, which is not what we want, which is why we need to do some extra work.
   564	                name === 'defaultValue' &&
   565	                (attributes.some(
   566	                        (attr) => attr.type === 'Attribute' && attr.name === 'value' && is_text_attribute(attr)
   567	                ) ||
   568	                        (element.name === 'textarea' && element.fragment.nodes.length > 0))
   569	        ) {
   570	                return b.call('$.set_default_value', node_id, value);
   571	        }
   572	
   573	        if (
   574	                // See defaultValue comment
   575	                name === 'defaultChecked' &&
   576	                attributes.some(
   577	                        (attr) => attr.type === 'Attribute' && attr.name === 'checked' && attr.value === true
   578	                )
   579	        ) {

    15	 * @param {AST.StyleDirective[]} style_directives

    18	 * @param {Identifier} element_id

    20	export function build_attribute_effect(
    21	        attributes,
    22	        class_directives,
    23	        style_directives,
    24	        context,
    25	        element,
    26	        element_id
    27	) {
    28	        /** @type {ObjectExpression['properties']} */
    29	        const values = [];
    30	
    31	        const memoizer = new Memoizer();
    32	
    33	        for (const attribute of attributes) {
    34	                if (attribute.type === 'Attribute') {
    35	                        const { value } = build_attribute_value(attribute.value, context, (value, metadata) =>
    36	                                metadata.has_call ? memoizer.add(value) : value
    37	                        );
    38	
    39	                        if (
    40	                                is_event_attribute(attribute) &&
    41	                                (value.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' || value.type === 'FunctionExpression')
    42	                        ) {
    43	                                // Give the event handler a stable ID so it isn't removed and readded on every update
    44	                                const id = context.state.scope.generate('event_handler');
    45	                                context.state.init.push(b.var(id, value));
    46	                                values.push(b.init(attribute.name, b.id(id)));
    47	                        } else {
    48	                                values.push(b.init(attribute.name, value));
    49	                        }
    50	                } else {
    51	                        let value = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(attribute));
    52	
    53	                        if (attribute.metadata.expression.has_call) {
    54	                                value = memoizer.add(value);
    55	                        }
    56	
    57	                        values.push(b.spread(value));
    58	                }
    59	        }
    60	
    61	        if (class_directives.length) {
    62	                values.push(
    63	                        b.prop(
    64	                                'init',
    65	                                b.array([b.id('$.CLASS')]),
    66	                                build_class_directives_object(class_directives, context, memoizer)
    67	                        )
    68	                );
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        if (style_directives.length) {
    72	                values.push(
    73	                        b.prop(
    74	                                'init',

    76	                                build_style_directives_object(style_directives, context, memoizer)
    77	                        )
    78	                );
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        const ids = memoizer.apply();

    99	/**
   100	 * @param {AST.Attribute['value']} value
   101	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   102	 * @param {(value: Expression, metadata: ExpressionMetadata) => Expression} memoize
   103	 * @returns {{ value: Expression, has_state: boolean }}
   104	 */
   105	export function build_attribute_value(value, context, memoize = (value) => value) {
   106	        if (value === true) {
   107	                return { value: b.true, has_state: false };
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        if (!Array.isArray(value) || value.length === 1) {
   111	                const chunk = Array.isArray(value) ? value[0] : value;
   112	
   113	                if (chunk.type === 'Text') {
   114	                        return { value: b.literal(chunk.data), has_state: false };
   115	                }
   116	
   117	                let expression = build_expression(context, chunk.expression, chunk.metadata.expression);
   118	
   119	                return {
   120	                        value: memoize(expression, chunk.metadata.expression),
   121	                        has_state: chunk.metadata.expression.has_state
   122	                };
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        return build_template_chunk(value, context, context.state, memoize);
   126	}
   127	
   128	/**
   129	 * @param {AST.RegularElement | AST.SvelteElement} element
   130	 * @param {AST.Attribute} attribute
   131	 */
   132	export function get_attribute_name(element, attribute) {
   133	        if (!element.metadata.svg && !element.metadata.mathml) {
   134	                return normalize_attribute(attribute.name);
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        return attribute.name;
   138	}

   148	export function build_set_class(element, node_id, attribute, class_directives, context, is_html) {
   149	        let { value, has_state } = build_attribute_value(attribute.value, context, (value, metadata) => {
   150	                if (attribute.metadata.needs_clsx) {
   151	                        value = b.call('$.clsx', value);
   152	                }
   153	
   154	                return metadata.has_call ? context.state.memoizer.add(value) : value;
   155	        });
   156	
   157	        /** @type {Identifier | undefined} */
   158	        let previous_id;
   159	
   160	        /** @type {ObjectExpression | Identifier | undefined} */
   161	        let prev;
   162	
   163	        /** @type {ObjectExpression | Identifier | undefined} */
   164	        let next;
   165	
   166	        if (class_directives.length) {
   167	                next = build_class_directives_object(class_directives, context);
   168	                has_state ||= class_directives.some((d) => d.metadata.expression.has_state);
   169

   171	                        previous_id = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('classes'));
   172	                        context.state.init.push(b.declaration('let', [b.declarator(previous_id)]));
   173	                        prev = previous_id;
   174	                } else {
   175	                        prev = b.object([]);
   176	                }
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        /** @type {Expression | undefined} */
   180	        let css_hash;
   181	
   182	        if (element.metadata.scoped && context.state.analysis.css.hash) {
   183	                if (value.type === 'Literal' && (value.value === '' || value.value === null)) {
   184	                        value = b.literal(context.state.analysis.css.hash);
   185	                } else if (value.type === 'Literal' && typeof value.value === 'string') {
   186	                        value = b.literal(escape_html(value.value, true) + ' ' + context.state.analysis.css.hash);
   187	                } else {
   188	                        css_hash = b.literal(context.state.analysis.css.hash);
   189	                }
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        if (!css_hash && next) {
   193	                css_hash = b.null;
   194	        }
   195	
   196	        /** @type {Expression} */
   197	        let set_class = b.call(
   198	                '$.set_class',
   199	                node_id,
   200	                is_html ? b.literal(1) : b.literal(0),
   201	                value,
   202	                css_hash,
   203	                prev,
   204	                next
   205	        );
   206	
   207	        if (previous_id) {
   208	                set_class = b.assignment('=', previous_id, set_class);
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        (has_state ? context.state.update : context.state.init).push(b.stmt(set_class));
   212	}

   214	/**

   220	export function build_set_style(node_id, attribute, style_directives, context) {
   221	        let { value, has_state } = build_attribute_value(attribute.value, context, (value, metadata) =>
   222	                metadata.has_call ? context.state.memoizer.add(value) : value
   223	        );

   225	        /** @type {Identifier | undefined} */
   226	        let previous_id;

   231	        /** @type {Expression | undefined} */
   232	        let next;

   234	        if (style_directives.length) {
   235	                next = build_style_directives_object(style_directives, context);
   236	                has_state ||= style_directives.some((d) => d.metadata.expression.has_state);

   242	                } else {
   243	                        prev = b.object([]);
   244	                }
   245	        }
   246	
   247	        /** @type {Expression} */
   248	        let set_style = b.call('$.set_style', node_id, value, prev, next);
   249	
   250	        if (previous_id) {
   251	                set_style = b.assignment('=', previous_id, set_style);
   252	        }
   253	
   254	        (has_state ? context.state.update : context.state.init).push(b.stmt(set_style));
   255	}
   256

    33	/**
    34	 * The value/checked attribute in the template actually corresponds to the defaultValue property, so we need
    35	 * to remove it upon hydration to avoid a bug when someone resets the form value.
    36	 * @param {HTMLInputElement} input
    37	 * @returns {void}
    38	 */
    39	export function remove_input_defaults(input) {
    40	        if (!hydrating) return;
    41	
    42	        var already_removed = false;
    43	
    44	        // We try and remove the default attributes later, rather than sync during hydration.
    45	        // Doing it sync during hydration has a negative impact on performance, but deferring the
    46	        // work in an idle task alleviates this greatly. If a form reset event comes in before
    47	        // the idle callback, then we ensure the input defaults are cleared just before.
    48	        var remove_defaults = () => {
    49	                if (already_removed) return;
    50	                already_removed = true;
    51	
    52	                // Remove the attributes but preserve the values
    53	                if (input.hasAttribute('value')) {
    54	                        var value = input.value;
    55	                        set_attribute(input, 'value', null);
    56	                        input.value = value;
    57	                }
    58	
    59	                if (input.hasAttribute('checked')) {
    60	                        var checked = input.checked;
    61	                        set_attribute(input, 'checked', null);
    62	                        input.checked = checked;
    63	                }
    64	        };
    65	
    66	        // @ts-expect-error
    67	        input.__on_r = remove_defaults;
    68	        queue_idle_task(remove_defaults);
    69	        add_form_reset_listener();
    70	}

    72	/**
    73	 * @param {Element} element
    74	 * @param {any} value
    75	 */
    76	export function set_value(element, value) {
    77	        var attributes = get_attributes(element);
    78	
    79	        if (
    80	                attributes.value ===
    81	                        (attributes.value =
    82	                                // treat null and undefined the same for the initial value
    83	                                value ?? undefined) ||
    84	                // @ts-expect-error
    85	                // `progress` elements always need their value set when it's `0`
    86	                (element.value === value && (value !== 0 || element.nodeName !== 'PROGRESS'))
    87	        ) {
    88	                return;
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        // @ts-expect-error
    92	        element.value = value ?? '';
    93	}

    99	export function set_checked(element, checked) {

   101	
   102	        if (
   103	                attributes.checked ===
   104	                (attributes.checked =
   105	                        // treat null and undefined the same for the initial value
   106	                        checked ?? undefined)
   107	        ) {
   108	                return;
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        // @ts-expect-error

   115	/**
   116	 * Sets the `selected` attribute on an `option` element.
   117	 * Not set through the property because that doesn't reflect to the DOM,
   118	 * which means it wouldn't be taken into account when a form is reset.
   119	 * @param {HTMLOptionElement} element
   120	 * @param {boolean} selected
   121	 */
   122	export function set_selected(element, selected) {
   123	        if (selected) {
   124	                // The selected option could've changed via user selection, and
   125	                // setting the value without this check would set it back.
   126	                if (!element.hasAttribute('selected')) {
   127	                        element.setAttribute('selected', '');
   128	                }
   129	        } else {
   130	                element.removeAttribute('selected');
   131	        }
   132	}

   140	        const existing_value = element.checked;
   141	        element.defaultChecked = checked;
   142	        element.checked = existing_value;

   150	export function set_default_value(element, value) {

   156	/**
   157	 * @param {Element} element
   158	 * @param {string} attribute
   159	 * @param {string | null} value
   160	 * @param {boolean} [skip_warning]
   161	 */
   162	export function set_attribute(element, attribute, value, skip_warning) {
   163	        var attributes = get_attributes(element);
   164	
   165	        if (hydrating) {
   166	                attributes[attribute] = element.getAttribute(attribute);
   167	
   168	                if (
   169	                        attribute === 'src' ||
   170	                        attribute === 'srcset' ||
   171	                        (attribute === 'href' && element.nodeName === 'LINK')
   172	                ) {
   173	                        if (!skip_warning) {
   174	                                check_src_in_dev_hydration(element, attribute, value ?? '');
   175	                        }
   176	
   177	                        // If we reset these attributes, they would result in another network request, which we want to avoid.
   178	                        // We assume they are the same between client and server as checking if they are equal is expensive
   179	                        // (we can't just compare the strings as they can be different between client and server but result in the
   180	                        // same url, so we would need to create hidden anchor elements to compare them)
   181	                        return;
   182	                }
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        if (attributes[attribute] === (attributes[attribute] = value)) return;
   186	
   187	        if (attribute === 'loading') {
   188	                // @ts-expect-error
   189	                element[LOADING_ATTR_SYMBOL] = value;
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        if (value == null) {
   193	                element.removeAttribute(attribute);
   194	        } else if (typeof value !== 'string' && get_setters(element).includes(attribute)) {
   195	                // @ts-ignore
   196	                element[attribute] = value;
   197	        } else {
   198	                element.setAttribute(attribute, value);
   199	        }
   200	}

   207	export function set_xlink_attribute(dom, attribute, value) {
   208	        dom.setAttributeNS('http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink', attribute, value);
   209	}

   211	/**
   212	 * @param {HTMLElement} node
   213	 * @param {string} prop
   214	 * @param {any} value
   215	 */
   216	export function set_custom_element_data(node, prop, value) {
   217	        // We need to ensure that setting custom element props, which can
   218	        // invoke lifecycle methods on other custom elements, does not also
   219	        // associate those lifecycle methods with the current active reaction
   220	        // or effect
   221	        var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   222	        var previous_effect = active_effect;
   223	
   224	        // If we're hydrating but the custom element is from Svelte, and it already scaffolded,
   225	        // then it might run block logic in hydration mode, which we have to prevent.
   226	        let was_hydrating = hydrating;
   227	        if (hydrating) {
   228	                set_hydrating(false);
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        set_active_reaction(null);
   232	        set_active_effect(null);
   233	
   234	        try {
   235	                if (
   236	                        // `style` should use `set_attribute` rather than the setter
   237	                        prop !== 'style' &&
   238	                        // Don't compute setters for custom elements while they aren't registered yet,
   239	                        // because during their upgrade/instantiation they might add more setters.
   240	                        // Instead, fall back to a simple "an object, then set as property" heuristic.
   241	                        (setters_cache.has(node.nodeName) ||
   242	                        // customElements may not be available in browser extension contexts
   243	                        !customElements ||
   244	                        customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase())
   245	                                ? get_setters(node).includes(prop)
   246	                                : value && typeof value === 'object')
   247	                ) {
   248	                        // @ts-expect-error
   249	                        node[prop] = value;
   250	                } else {
   251	                        // We did getters etc checks already, stringify before passing to set_attribute
   252	                        // to ensure it doesn't invoke the same logic again, and potentially populating
   253	                        // the setters cache too early.
   254	                        set_attribute(node, prop, value == null ? value : String(value));
   255	                }
   256	        } finally {
   257	                set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
   258	                set_active_effect(previous_effect);
   259	                if (was_hydrating) {
   260	                        set_hydrating(true);
   261	                }
   262	        }
   263	}
   264	
   265	/**
   266	 * Spreads attributes onto a DOM element, taking into account the currently set attributes
   267	 * @param {Element & ElementCSSInlineStyle} element
   268	 * @param {Record<string | symbol, any> | undefined} prev
   269	 * @param {Record<string | symbol, any>} next New attributes - this function mutates this object
   270	 * @param {string} [css_hash]
   271	 * @param {boolean} [skip_warning]
   272	 * @returns {Record<string, any>}
   273	 */
   274	export function set_attributes(element, prev, next, css_hash, skip_warning = false) {
   275	        var attributes = get_attributes(element);
   276	
   277	        var is_custom_element = attributes[IS_CUSTOM_ELEMENT];
   278	        var preserve_attribute_case = !attributes[IS_HTML];
   279	
   280	        // If we're hydrating but the custom element is from Svelte, and it already scaffolded,
   281	        // then it might run block logic in hydration mode, which we have to prevent.
   282	        let is_hydrating_custom_element = hydrating && is_custom_element;
   283	        if (is_hydrating_custom_element) {
   284	                set_hydrating(false);
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        var current = prev || {};
   288	        var is_option_element = element.tagName === 'OPTION';
   289	
   290	        for (var key in prev) {
   291	                if (!(key in next)) {
   292	                        next[key] = null;
   293	                }
   294	        }
   295	
   296	        if (next.class) {
   297	                next.class = clsx(next.class);
   298	        } else if (css_hash || next[CLASS]) {
   299	                next.class = null; /* force call to set_class() */
   300	        }
   301	
   302	        if (next[STYLE]) {
   303	                next.style ??= null; /* force call to set_style() */
   304	        }
   305	
   306	        var setters = get_setters(element);
   307	
   308	        // since key is captured we use const
   309	        for (const key in next) {
   310	                // let instead of var because referenced in a closure
   311	                let value = next[key];
   312	
   313	                // Up here because we want to do this for the initial value, too, even if it's undefined,
   314	                // and this wouldn't be reached in case of undefined because of the equality check below
   315	                if (is_option_element && key === 'value' && value == null) {
   316	                        // The <option> element is a special case because removing the value attribute means
   317	                        // the value is set to the text content of the option element, and setting the value
   318	                        // to null or undefined means the value is set to the string "null" or "undefined".
   319	                        // To align with how we handle this case in non-spread-scenarios, this logic is needed.
   320	                        // There's a super-edge-case bug here that is left in in favor of smaller code size:
   321	                        // Because of the "set missing props to null" logic above, we can't differentiate
   322	                        // between a missing value and an explicitly set value of null or undefined. That means
   323	                        // that once set, the value attribute of an <option> element can't be removed. This is
   324	                        // a very rare edge case, and removing the attribute altogether isn't possible either
   325	                        // for the <option value={undefined}> case, so we're not losing any functionality here.
   326	                        // @ts-ignore
   327	                        element.value = element.__value = '';
   328	                        current[key] = value;
   329	                        continue;
   330	                }
   331	
   332	                if (key === 'class') {
   333	                        var is_html = element.namespaceURI === 'http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml';
   334	                        set_class(element, is_html, value, css_hash, prev?.[CLASS], next[CLASS]);
   335	                        current[key] = value;
   336	                        current[CLASS] = next[CLASS];
   337	                        continue;
   338	                }
   339	
   340	                if (key === 'style') {
   341	                        set_style(element, value, prev?.[STYLE], next[STYLE]);
   342	                        current[key] = value;
   343	                        current[STYLE] = next[STYLE];
   344	                        continue;
   345	                }
   346	
   347	                var prev_value = current[key];
   348	
   349	                // Skip if value is unchanged, unless it's `undefined` and the element still has the attribute
   350	                if (value === prev_value && !(value === undefined && element.hasAttribute(key))) {
   351	                        continue;
   352	                }
   353	
   354	                current[key] = value;
   355	
   356	                var prefix = key[0] + key[1]; // this is faster than key.slice(0, 2)
   357	                if (prefix === '$$') continue;
   358	
   359	                if (prefix === 'on') {
   360	                        /** @type {{ capture?: true }} */
   361	                        const opts = {};
   362	                        const event_handle_key = '$$' + key;
   363	                        let event_name = key.slice(2);
   364	                        var delegated = is_delegated(event_name);
   365	
   366	                        if (is_capture_event(event_name)) {
   367	                                event_name = event_name.slice(0, -7);
   368	                                opts.capture = true;
   369	                        }
   370	
   371	                        if (!delegated && prev_value) {
   372	                                // Listening to same event but different handler -> our handle function below takes care of this
   373	                                // If we were to remove and add listeners in this case, it could happen that the event is "swallowed"
   374	                                // (the browser seems to not know yet that a new one exists now) and doesn't reach the handler
   375	                                // https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/11903
   376	                                if (value != null) continue;
   377	
   378	                                element.removeEventListener(event_name, current[event_handle_key], opts);
   379	                                current[event_handle_key] = null;
   380	                        }
   381	
   382	                        if (value != null) {
   383	                                if (!delegated) {
   384	                                        /**
   385	                                         * @this {any}
   386	                                         * @param {Event} evt
   387	                                         */
   388	                                        function handle(evt) {
   389	                                                current[key].call(this, evt);
   390	                                        }
   391	
   392	                                        current[event_handle_key] = create_event(event_name, element, handle, opts);
   393	                                } else {
   394	                                        // @ts-ignore
   395	                                        element[`__${event_name}`] = value;
   396	                                        delegate([event_name]);
   397	                                }
   398	                        } else if (delegated) {
   399	                                // @ts-ignore
   400	                                element[`__${event_name}`] = undefined;
   401	                        }
   402	                } else if (key === 'style') {
   403	                        // avoid using the setter
   404	                        set_attribute(element, key, value);
   405	                } else if (key === 'autofocus') {
   406	                        autofocus(/** @type {HTMLElement} */ (element), Boolean(value));
   407	                } else if (!is_custom_element && (key === '__value' || (key === 'value' && value != null))) {
   408	                        // @ts-ignore We're not running this for custom elements because __value is actually
   409	                        // how Lit stores the current value on the element, and messing with that would break things.
   410	                        element.value = element.__value = value;
   411	                } else if (key === 'selected' && is_option_element) {
   412	                        set_selected(/** @type {HTMLOptionElement} */ (element), value);
   413	                } else {
   414	                        var name = key;
   415	                        if (!preserve_attribute_case) {
   416	                                name = normalize_attribute(name);
   417	                        }
   418	
   419	                        var is_default = name === 'defaultValue' || name === 'defaultChecked';
   420	
   421	                        if (value == null && !is_custom_element && !is_default) {
   422	                                attributes[key] = null;
   423	
   424	                                if (name === 'value' || name === 'checked') {
   425	                                        // removing value/checked also removes defaultValue/defaultChecked — preserve
   426	                                        let input = /** @type {HTMLInputElement} */ (element);
   427	                                        const use_default = prev === undefined;
   428	                                        if (name === 'value') {
   429	                                                let previous = input.defaultValue;
   430	                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
   431	                                                input.defaultValue = previous;
   432	                                                // @ts-ignore
   433	                                                input.value = input.__value = use_default ? previous : null;
   434	                                        } else {
   435	                                                let previous = input.defaultChecked;
   436	                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
   437	                                                input.defaultChecked = previous;
   438	                                                input.checked = use_default ? previous : false;
   439	                                        }
   440	                                } else {
   441	                                        element.removeAttribute(key);
   442	                                }
   443	                        } else if (
   444	                                is_default ||

   469	export function attribute_effect(
   470	        element,
   471	        fn,
   472	        thunks = [],
   473	        css_hash,
   474	        skip_warning = false,
   475	        d = derived
   476	) {
   477	        const deriveds = thunks.map(d);
   478	
   479	        /** @type {Record<string | symbol, any> | undefined} */
   480	        var prev = undefined;
   481	
   482	        /** @type {Record<symbol, Effect>} */
   483	        var effects = {};
   484	
   485	        var is_select = element.nodeName === 'SELECT';
   486	        var inited = false;
   487	
   488	        block(() => {
   489	                var next = fn(...deriveds.map(get));
   490	                /** @type {Record<string | symbol, any>} */
   491	                var current = set_attributes(element, prev, next, css_hash, skip_warning);
   492	
   493	                if (inited && is_select && 'value' in next) {
   494	                        select_option(/** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element), next.value, false);
   495	                }
   496	
   497	                for (let symbol of Object.getOwnPropertySymbols(effects)) {
   498	                        if (!next[symbol]) destroy_effect(effects[symbol]);
   499	                }
   500	
   501	                for (let symbol of Object.getOwnPropertySymbols(next)) {
   502	                        var n = next[symbol];
   503	
   504	                        if (symbol.description === ATTACHMENT_KEY && (!prev || n !== prev[symbol])) {
   505	                                if (effects[symbol]) destroy_effect(effects[symbol]);
   506	                                effects[symbol] = branch(() => attach(element, () => n));
   507	                        }
   508	
   509	                        current[symbol] = n;
   510	                }
   511	
   512	                prev = current;
   513	        });
   514	
   515	        if (is_select) {
   516	                var select = /** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element);
   517	
   518	                effect(() => {
   519	                        select_option(select, /** @type {Record<string | symbol, any>} */ (prev).value);
   520	                        init_select(select);
   521	                });
   522	        }
   523	
   524	        inited = true;
   525	}

     1	import { effect, teardown } from '../../../reactivity/effects.js';
     2	import { listen_to_event_and_reset_event } from './shared.js';
     3	import { is } from '../../../proxy.js';
     4	import { is_array } from '../../../../shared/utils.js';
     5	import * as w from '../../../warnings.js';
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Selects the correct option(s) (depending on whether this is a multiple select)
     9	 * @template V
    10	 * @param {HTMLSelectElement} select
    11	 * @param {V} value
    12	 * @param {boolean} [mounting]
    13	 */
    14	export function select_option(select, value, mounting) {
    15	        if (select.multiple) {
    16	                // If value is null or undefined, keep the selection as is
    17	                if (value == undefined) {
    18	                        return;
    19	                }
    20	
    21	                // If not an array, warn and keep the selection as is
    22	                if (!is_array(value)) {
    23	                        return w.select_multiple_invalid_value();
    24	                }
    25	
    26	                // Otherwise, update the selection
    27	                for (var option of select.options) {
    28	                        option.selected = value.includes(get_option_value(option));
    29	                }
    30	
    31	                return;
    32	        }
    33	
    34	        for (option of select.options) {
    35	                var option_value = get_option_value(option);
    36	                if (is(option_value, value)) {
    37	                        option.selected = true;
    38	                        return;
    39	                }
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        if (!mounting || value !== undefined) {
    43	                select.selectedIndex = -1; // no option should be selected
    44	        }
    45	}
    46	
    47	/**
    48	 * Selects the correct option(s) if `value` is given,
    49	 * and then sets up a mutation observer to sync the
    50	 * current selection to the dom when it changes. Such
    51	 * changes could for example occur when options are
    52	 * inside an `#each` block.
    53	 * @param {HTMLSelectElement} select
    54	 */
    55	export function init_select(select) {
    56	        var observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
    57	                // @ts-ignore
    58	                select_option(select, select.__value);
    59	                // Deliberately don't update the potential binding value,
    60	                // the model should be preserved unless explicitly changed
    61	        });
    62	
    63	        observer.observe(select, {
    64	                // Listen to option element changes
    65	                childList: true,
    66	                subtree: true, // because of <optgroup>
    67	                // Listen to option element value attribute changes
    68	                // (doesn't get notified of select value changes,
    69	                // because that property is not reflected as an attribute)
    70	                attributes: true,
    71	                attributeFilter: ['value']
    72	        });
    73	
    74	        teardown(() => {
    75	                observer.disconnect();
    76	        });
    77	}
    78	
    79	/**
    80	 * @param {HTMLSelectElement} select
    81	 * @param {() => unknown} get
    82	 * @param {(value: unknown) => void} set
    83	 * @returns {void}
    84	 */
    85	export function bind_select_value(select, get, set = get) {
    86	        var mounting = true;
    87	
    88	        listen_to_event_and_reset_event(select, 'change', (is_reset) => {
    89	                var query = is_reset ? '[selected]' : ':checked';
    90	                /** @type {unknown} */
    91	                var value;
    92	
    93	                if (select.multiple) {
    94	                        value = [].map.call(select.querySelectorAll(query), get_option_value);
    95	                } else {
    96	                        /** @type {HTMLOptionElement | null} */
    97	                        var selected_option =
    98	                                select.querySelector(query) ??
    99	                                // will fall back to first non-disabled option if no option is selected
   100	                                select.querySelector('option:not([disabled])');
   101	                        value = selected_option && get_option_value(selected_option);
   102	                }
   103	
   104	                set(value);
   105	        });
   106	
   107	        // Needs to be an effect, not a render_effect, so that in case of each loops the logic runs after the each block has updated
   108	        effect(() => {
   109	                var value = get();
   110	                select_option(select, value, mounting);
   111	
   112	                // Mounting and value undefined -> take selection from dom
   113	                if (mounting && value === undefined) {
   114	                        /** @type {HTMLOptionElement | null} */
   115	                        var selected_option = select.querySelector(':checked');
   116	                        if (selected_option !== null) {
   117	                                value = get_option_value(selected_option);
   118	                                set(value);
   119	                        }
   120	                }
   121	
   122	                // @ts-ignore
   123	                select.__value = value;
   124	                mounting = false;
   125	        });
   126	
   127	        init_select(select);
   128	}
   129	
   130	/** @param {HTMLOptionElement} option */
   131	function get_option_value(option) {
   132	        // __value only exists if the <option> has a value attribute
   133	        if ('__value' in option) {
   134	                return option.__value;
   135	        } else {
   136	                return option.value;
   137	        }
   138	}
   139

```javascript
var root = $.from_html(`<select id="select1"><option>o1</option><option selected>o2</option></select> <select><option>o1</option><option selected>o2</option></select>`, 1);
```


    20	                 * @param {any} value
    21	                 */
    22	                function set_input(input, field, value) {
    23	                        input[field] = value;
    24	                        input.dispatchEvent(
    25	                                new Event(typeof value === 'boolean' ? 'change' : 'input', { bubbles: true })
    26	                        );
    27	                }
    28	
    29	                /**
    30	                 * @param {HTMLOptionElement} option
    31	                 */
    32	                function select_option(option) {
    33	                        option.selected = true;
    34	                        option.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
    35	                }
    36	
    37	                const after_reset = [];

2025-12-26 22:19:14,824 - INFO - swea-agent-sveltejs__svelte-16309 - 💭 THOUGHT
Perfect! Now I can see the issue. When `$.attribute_effect` is called, it's spreading the attributes which means it will call `set_attributes`. Looking back at the `attribute_effect` function in `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/dom/elements/attributes.js`, I see that on line 485 it checks `var is_select = element.nodeName === 'SELECT';` and then lines 515-522 set up the `select_option` function for select elements.

However, the issue is that when `set_attributes` is called initially (on line 491), it resets attributes based on what's passed in `next`. The `selected` attribute is in the template but not being passed through the spread.

Let me look more closely at the logic. The key is in the `attribute_effect` function:

```javascript
block(() => {
    var next = fn(...deriveds.map(get));
    var current = set_attributes(element, prev, next, css_hash, skip_warning);
    
    if (inited && is_select && 'value' in next) {
        select_option(/** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element), next.value, false);
    }
    
    // ... rest of code
    prev = current;
});

if (is_select) {
    var select = /** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element);
    
    effect(() => {
        select_option(select, /** @type {Record<string | symbol, any>} */ (prev).value);
        init_select(select);
    });
}

inited = true;
```

The problem is that `selected` attribute is being set in the template HTML, but when `set_attributes` is called for the first time with the spread, it doesn't preserve the selected state of the options that were already set in the template.

Looking at the `set_attributes` function around line 411:

```javascript
} else if (key === 'selected' && is_option_element) {
    set_selected(/** @type {HTMLOptionElement} */ (element), value);
```

This only applies to option elements, but the issue is that the select element has spread attributes and the options inside it have the `selected` attribute set in the template.

The root cause is that when a select element has a spread, the `attribute_effect` is called, and within that, the initial HTML includes options with `selected` attributes. But since there's no code to preserve these initial selected states when the spread is applied, they get lost.

Let me look at what happens with option elements when there's no spread vs. with spread. Looking back at the template output:

```html
<select><option>o1</option><option selected>o2</option></select>
```

This is in the template, so the option should initially have the selected attribute. But when `attribute_effect` is called on the select, it doesn't do anything to preserve or restore the initial selected state of its options.

Let me check the `attribute_effect` function more carefully. At line 515-522:

```javascript
if (is_select) {
    var select = /** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element);
    
    effect(() => {
        select_option(select, /** @type {Record<string | symbol, any>} */ (prev).value);
        init_select(select);
    });
}
```

The issue is that `prev.value` is `undefined` initially because the spread object doesn't have a `value` property. So `select_option` is called with `undefined` value, and according to the `select_option` function:

```javascript
export function select_option(select, value, mounting) {
    if (select.multiple) {
        // If value is null or undefined, keep the selection as is
        if (value == undefined) {
            return;
        }
        // ...
    }
    
    for (option of select.options) {
        var option_value = get_option_value(option);
        if (is(option_value, value)) {
            option.selected = true;
            return;
        }
    }
    
    if (!mounting || value !== undefined) {
        select.selectedIndex = -1; // no option should be selected
    }
}
```

When `value` is `undefined` and `mounting` is `false` (which would be after init since the effect runs after the block), it doesn't set `selectedIndex = -1` according to the condition `if (!mounting || value !== undefined)`.

Wait, let me re-read this. The condition is `if (!mounting || value !== undefined)`. So:
- If `mounting` is false, then `!mounting` is true, so the condition is true -> selectedIndex = -1
- If `value !== undefined`, the condition is true -> selectedIndex = -1

So if `value` is `undefined` during mounting, it should not set `selectedIndex = -1`. But if it's not mounting and value is undefined, it would set `selectedIndex = -1` which is the bug!

Actually, looking at the logic flow:
1. The template HTML includes `<option selected>o2</option>`
2. `attribute_effect` is called
3. Inside the `block()`, `set_attributes` is called
4. Then later, the `effect()` is set up which calls `select_option`
5. The `inited = true` is set AFTER both the block and effect

So the sequence is:
1. Template is created with selected attribute
2. `block()` runs: `set_attributes` is called (but doesn't touch option's selected attribute since it's not in the spread)
3. `effect()` is set up: this will call `select_option(select, undefined)` because `prev.value` is undefined
4. `inited = true`

When `select_option` is called with `undefined` value inside the effect, the `mounting` parameter is not passed, so it defaults to `undefined`. Let me check:

```javascript
effect(() => {
    select_option(select, /** @type {Record<string | symbol, any>} */ (prev).value);
    init_select(select);
});
```

Yes, `select_option` is called with only 2 arguments (select and value), so `mounting` would be `undefined`.

In `select_option`:
```javascript
export function select_option(select, value, mounting) {
    if (select.multiple) {
        if (value == undefined) {
            return;
        }
        // ...
    }
    
    for (option of select.options) {
        var option_value = get_option_value(option);
        if (is(option_value, value)) {
            option.selected = true;
            return;
        }
    }
    
    if (!mounting || value !== undefined) {
        select.selectedIndex = -1; // no option should be selected
    }
}
```

So if `value` is `undefined` and `mounting` is `undefined`:
- The loop runs through all options
- None of them match `undefined` (since `is(option_value, undefined)` would be false for 'o1' and 'o2')
- Then it hits the condition: `if (!mounting || value !== undefined)`
  - `!mounting` = `!undefined` = `true`
  - So the condition is true and `select.selectedIndex = -1` is executed!

This is the bug! When there's a spread on a select element, the `attribute_effect` sets up an effect that calls `select_option` with `undefined` value and `undefined` mounting, which causes it to clear the selection that was set in the template.

The fix should be to either:
1. Pass `mounting: true` or some flag to preserve the initial selection when value is undefined
2. Not call `select_option` at all when value is undefined and we're in the initial render
3. Read the initial selected state before calling `select_option`

Let me look at how this is handled in the case without spread. Looking back at `RegularElement.js`:

```javascript
if (node.name === 'select' && bindings.has('value')) {
    setup_select_synchronization(/** @type {AST.BindDirective} */ (bindings.get('value')), context);
}
```

So if there's a `bind:value`, special synchronization is set up. But in our case, there's no binding, just a selected attribute on an option.

Looking at when `select_option` is called from `bind_select_value`:

```javascript
export function bind_select_value(select, get, set = get) {
    var mounting = true;
    
    // ...
    
    effect(() => {
        var value = get();
        select_option(select, value, mounting);
        
        // Mounting and value undefined -> take selection from dom
        if (mounting && value === undefined) {
            /** @type {HTMLOptionElement | null} */
            var selected_option = select.querySelector(':checked');
            if (selected_option !== null) {
                value = get_option_value(selected_option);
                set(value);
            }
        }
        
        // @ts-ignore
        select.__value = value;
        mounting = false;
    });
    
    init_select(select);
}
```

Here, `mounting` starts as `true` and is set to `false` after the first run. This ensures that on the first run, if `value` is `undefined`, it doesn't clear the selection.

So the fix should be to do the same in `attribute_effect` when dealing with select elements. Let me look at the code again:

```javascript
var is_select = element.nodeName === 'SELECT';
var inited = false;

block(() => {
    var next = fn(...deriveds.map(get));
    var current = set_attributes(element, prev, next, css_hash, skip_warning);
    
    if (inited && is_select && 'value' in next) {
        select_option(/** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element), next.value, false);
    }
    
    // ... rest
    prev = current;
});

if (is_select) {
    var select = /** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element);
    
    effect(() => {
        select_option(select, /** @type {Record<string | symbol, any>} */ (prev).value);
        init_select(select);
    });
}

inited = true;
```

The issue is in the `effect()` call. It should pass `true` for the `mounting` parameter on the first run. Let me draft a fix:

   494	                        select_option(/** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element), next.value, false);
   495	                }
   496

   498	                        if (!next[symbol]) destroy_effect(effects[symbol]);
   499	                }
   500	
   501	                for (let symbol of Object.getOwnPropertySymbols(next)) {
   502	                        var n = next[symbol];
   503	
   504	                        if (symbol.description === ATTACHMENT_KEY && (!prev || n !== prev[symbol])) {
   505	                                if (effects[symbol]) destroy_effect(effects[symbol]);
   506	                                effects[symbol] = branch(() => attach(element, () => n));
   507	                        }
   508	
   509	                        current[symbol] = n;
   510	                }
   511	
   512	                prev = current;
   513	        });

   516	                var select = /** @type {HTMLSelectElement} */ (element);
   517

   519	                        select_option(select, /** @type {Record<string | symbol, any>} */ (prev).value);
   520	                        init_select(select);
   521	                });
   522	        }
   523	
   524	        inited = true;
   525	}

   530	 */
